  <script>
   //$('#widget').draggable();

$(function() {


    alignMenu();

    $(window).resize(function() {
        $("#horizontal").append($("#horizontal li.hideshow ul").html());
        $("#horizontal li.hideshow").remove();
        alignMenu();
    });


    function alignMenu() {

        var w = 0;
        var mw = $("#horizontal").width() - 150;
        var i = -1;
        var menuhtml = '';
        jQuery.each($("#horizontal").children(), function() {
            i++;
            w += $(this).outerWidth(true);
            if (mw &lt; w) {
                menuhtml += $('&lt;div&gt;').append($(this).clone()).html();
                $(this).remove();
            }
        });
        $("#horizontal").append(
            '&lt;li  style="position:relative;" href="#" class="hideshow"&gt;'
            + '&lt;a href="#"&gt; '
            + '&lt;span style="font-size:13px"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'
            + '&lt;/a&gt;&lt;ul&gt;' + menuhtml + '&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/li&gt;');
        $("#horizontal li.hideshow ul").css("top",
            $("#horizontal li.hideshow").outerHeight(true) + "px");
        $("#horizontal li.hideshow").click(function() {
            $(this).children("ul").toggle();
        });
        if (menuhtml == '') {
            $("#horizontal li.hideshow").hide();
        } else {
            $("#horizontal li.hideshow").show();
        }
    }


});
  </script>

   $(document).ready(	function ()
    {
		
		$("#logout").click(function() 
			{ 
			//var email = $("#email_val").val();
			//alert(email);
			
					
					$.ajax({
						  url: "http://www.crazydeals.com/user/logout"
						})
						  .done(function( msg ) {
							  
							 location.reload();
		
					  });
					  
			  }); // click end


        $(".field_reg_pop_register_but").click(function(event)
        {

            event.preventDefault();
            var user_email = $("#username").val();
            var user_pwd = $("#user_password").val();

            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "http://www.crazydeals.com/user/ajax_user_login_validate",
                data: { username: user_email,password: user_pwd }

            })
                .done(function( msg ) {
                    if(msg.trim()==1)
                    {
                        location.reload();
                    }else if(msg.trim()==0 || msg.trim()==2){
                        $(".show_user_login_error").css('display',"block");
                    }

                });

        }); // click end



    $('.fancybox').fancybox();
    $('#submit_req_call').click(function(){
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: "http://www.crazydeals.com/request_callback/request_call_back",
            data: { name_cl_rq: $("#name_req_call").val(),mobile_cl_rq: $('#mobile_req_call').val(),email_cl_rq:$('#email_req_call').val(),comment_cl_rq:$('#comment_req_call').val() }
        }).done(function( msg ) {

            if(msg == 1)
            {
                $("#error").html('Please enter a valid Email Address');
                $("#succes").html('');
                return false;
            }
            if(msg == 2)
            {

                $("#error").html('This email is already registered.!');
                $("#succes").html('');
                return false;
            }
            if(msg == 3)
            {


                $(".thank_you_rc").show();
                $('.s6_form').hide();
                setTimeout(function() {
                    location.reload();
                }, 10000);

                return false;
            }
        });
    });

    });

  <script>
   $(document).ready(function() {
    $( '.active' ).hover(
        function(){
            $(this).children('.dropdown-menu').slideDown(200);
        },
        function(){
            $(this).children('.dropdown-menu').slideUp(200);
        }
    );


});
        var $menu = $(".dropdown-menu");
       
        // jQuery-menu-aim: &lt;meaningful part of the example&gt;
        // Hook up events to be fired on menu row activation.
        $menu.menuAim({
            activate: activateSubmenu,
            deactivate: deactivateSubmenu
        });
        // jQuery-menu-aim: &lt;/meaningful part of the example&gt;

        // jQuery-menu-aim: the following JS is used to show and hide the submenu
        // contents. Again, this can be done in any number of ways. jQuery-menu-aim
        // doesn't care how you do this, it just fires the activate and deactivate
        // events at the right times so you know when to show and hide your submenus.
        function activateSubmenu(row) {
            var $row = $(row),
                submenuId = $row.data("submenuId"),
                $submenu = $("#" + submenuId),
                height = $menu.outerHeight(),
                width = $menu.outerWidth();

            // Show the submenu
            $submenu.css({
                display: "block",
                top: -1,
                left: width - 3,  // main should overlay submenu
                height: "auto"
				   // padding for main dropdown's arrow
            });

            // Keep the currently activated row's highlighted look
            $row.find("a").addClass("maintainHover");
        }

        function deactivateSubmenu(row) {
            var $row = $(row),
                submenuId = $row.data("submenuId"),
                $submenu = $("#" + submenuId);

            // Hide the submenu and remove the row's highlighted look
            $submenu.css("display", "none");
            $row.find("a").removeClass("maintainHover");
        }

        // Bootstrap's dropdown menus immediately close on document click.
        // Don't let this event close the menu if a submenu is being clicked.
        // This event propagation control doesn't belong in the menu-aim plugin
        // itself because the plugin is agnostic to bootstrap.
        $(".dropdown-menu li").click(function(e) {
            e.stopPropagation();
        });

        $(document).click(function() {
            // Simply hide the submenu on any click. Again, this is just a hacked
            // together menu/submenu structure to show the use of jQuery-menu-aim.
            $(".popover").css("display", "none");
            $("a.maintainHover").removeClass("maintainHover");
        });
  </script>

  <script>
   $(document).ready(function(){
	
	
	//Logout
	
	
			  
			  
	// ajax for news letter
			$(".newsletter_bttn").click(function() 
			{ 
			//var email = $("#email_val").val();
			//alert(email);
			
					$(".email_n_response").html('&lt;img src="http://www.crazydeals.com/assets/images/ajax-loader.gif" /&gt; ');
					$.ajax({
						  type: "POST",
						  url: "http://www.crazydeals.com/ajax/newsletter",
						  data: { email_n: $("#email_val").val() }
						})
						  .done(function( msg ) {
							 
						  
						$(".footer-email").css('display','block');
						$(".email_n_response").html(msg);
								
						$('.email_n_response').delay(3000).fadeOut('slow');	
						
		
					  });
					  
			  }); // click end
										
	
	
		$('.hover_cat').hover(function(){
			var cat_id = $(this).attr('id');
			var mod_id = cat_id % 6;
			switch(mod_id)
			{
				case 1: var col ='#ef8168';break;
				case 2:var col = '#63a69f';break;
				case 3:var col = '#7573b4';break;
				case 4:var col = '#fec31d';break;
				case 5:var col = '#a1cd38';break;
				case 0:var col = '#00adef';break;
			}
			
			$('.hover_'+cat_id).css('color',col);
			$('.hover_'+cat_id+'_hover').css('background-color',col);
			
			
		});
		$('.hover_cat').mouseleave(function(e) {
			var cat_id1 = $(this).attr('id');
            $('.hover_'+cat_id1+'_hover').css('background-color','#FFF');
        });
		
		

		$("#back-top").hide();
		
		// fade in #back-top
		$(function () {
			$(window).scroll(function () {
				if ($(this).scrollTop() &gt; 100) {
					$('#back-top').fadeIn();
				} else {
					$('#back-top').fadeOut();
				}
			});
	
			// scroll body to 0px on click
			$('#back-top a').click(function () {
				$('body,html').animate({
					scrollTop: 0
				}, 800);
				return false;
			});
		});
	});
  </script>
  <script>
   function toggleCodes(on) {
        var obj = document.getElementById('icons');
        
        if (on) {
          obj.className += ' codesOn';
        } else {
          obj.className = obj.className.replace(' codesOn', '');
        }
      }
